================================================================
File Summary
================================================================

Purpose:
--------
This file contains a packed representation of the entire repository's contents.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:
------------
The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section
2. Repository information
3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.

Notes:
------
- Some files may have been excluded based on .gitignore rules and Repomix's configuration
- Binary files are not included in this packed representation. Please refer to the Repository Structure section for a complete list of file paths, including binary files
- Files matching patterns in .gitignore are excluded
- Files matching default ignore patterns are excluded
- Files are sorted by Git change count (files with more changes are at the bottom)

================
File: assets/js/dashboard.js

const DATA_PATH = 'outputs/table-results.json';
const DEFAULT_SECTOR = 'Differently Abled';
const LIST_LIMIT = 35;
const PINCODE_REGEX = /\b\d{6}\b/;
const PINCODE_DATA_PATH = 'assets/data/pincode-locations.json';
const MAX_LOCATION_SCAN = 30;
let pincodeLocations = {};
let isPincodeMapLoaded = false;
let hasPincodeMapError = false;

const elements = {
  captureTimestamp: document.getElementById('capture-timestamp'),
  selectionLocation: document.getElementById('selection-location'),
  datasetCount: document.getElementById('dataset-count'),
  datasetAverage: document.getElementById('dataset-average'),
  datasetSectors: document.getElementById('dataset-sectors'),
  sectorOptions: document.getElementById('sector-options'),
  selectedSectors: document.getElementById('selected-sectors'),
  filteredCount: document.getElementById('filtered-count'),
  filteredNote: document.getElementById('filtered-note'),
  currentAverage: document.getElementById('current-average'),
  topPairings: document.getElementById('top-pairings'),
  sectorChart: document.getElementById('sector-chart'),
  chartCount: document.getElementById('chart-count'),
  ngoList: document.getElementById('ngo-list'),
  listMessage: document.getElementById('list-message'),
  resultCount: document.getElementById('result-count'),
  listLimit: document.getElementById('list-limit'),
  errorMessage: document.getElementById('error-message'),
  sectorSearch: document.getElementById('sector-search'),
  ngoSearch: document.getElementById('ngo-search'),
  resetButton: document.getElementById('reset-filters'),
  filterNote: document.getElementById('filter-note'),
  pairedList: document.getElementById('top-pairings'),
  locationBadge: document.getElementById('location-badge'),
  locationPincodes: document.getElementById('location-pincodes'),
  locationDistance: document.getElementById('location-distance'),
  locationPairs: document.getElementById('location-pairs'),
  locationClosest: document.getElementById('location-closest'),
};

let datasetRows = [];
let datasetSectorList = [];
let selectedSectors = new Set([DEFAULT_SECTOR]);
let searchTerm = '';
let sectorSearchTerm = '';

async function init() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(DATA_PATH);
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Status ${response.status}`);
    }
    const payload = await response.json();
    const selections = payload.selections ?? {};
    const rows = Array.isArray(payload.table?.rows) ? payload.table.rows : [];

    elements.captureTimestamp.textContent = payload.capturedAt
      ? new Date(payload.capturedAt).toLocaleString()
      : '—';
    elements.selectionLocation.textContent = `${selections.selectedState ?? '—'} / ${
      selections.selectedDistrict ?? '—'
    }`;

    datasetRows = rows.map((row) => {
      const rawSectors = (row['Sectors working in'] ?? '')
        .split(',')
        .map((value) => value.trim())
        .filter(Boolean);
      return {
        ...row,
        sectors: rawSectors,
        searchable: `${row['Name of NPO'] ?? ''} ${row.Address ?? ''}`.toLowerCase(),
      };
    });

    elements.datasetCount.textContent = datasetRows.length.toLocaleString();
    const datasetAverage =
      datasetRows.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.sectors.length, 0) / (datasetRows.length || 1);
    elements.datasetAverage.textContent = datasetRows.length ? datasetAverage.toFixed(2) : '0';
    datasetSectorList = computeSectorCounts(datasetRows);
    elements.datasetSectors.textContent = datasetSectorList.length.toString();

    await loadPincodeMap();

    setupControls();
    updateView();
  } catch (error) {
    showError(`Unable to load dashboard data. Make sure ${DATA_PATH} is accessible (${error.message}).`);
  }
}

function setupControls() {
  elements.sectorSearch.addEventListener('input', (event) => {
    sectorSearchTerm = event.target.value;
    renderSectorButtons();
  });

  elements.ngoSearch.addEventListener('input', (event) => {
    searchTerm = event.target.value.trim().toLowerCase();
    updateView();
  });

  elements.resetButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
    selectedSectors = new Set([DEFAULT_SECTOR]);
    searchTerm = '';
    sectorSearchTerm = '';
    elements.ngoSearch.value = '';
    elements.sectorSearch.value = '';
    updateView();
  });

  renderSectorButtons();
}

function computeSectorCounts(rows) {
  const counts = new Map();
  rows.forEach((row) => {
    row.sectors.forEach((sector) => {
      counts.set(sector, (counts.get(sector) || 0) + 1);
    });
  });
  return [...counts.entries()]
    .map(([name, count]) => ({ name, count }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count || a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
}

function getFilteredRows() {
  const activeSectors = Array.from(selectedSectors);
  return datasetRows.filter((row) => {
    const hasAllSectors = activeSectors.every((sector) => row.sectors.includes(sector));
    if (!hasAllSectors) {
      return false;
    }
    if (!searchTerm) {
      return true;
    }
    return row.searchable.includes(searchTerm);
  });
}

function updateView() {
  const filteredRows = getFilteredRows();
  renderStats(filteredRows);
  renderSectorChart(filteredRows);
  renderList(filteredRows);
  renderTopPairings(filteredRows);
  void renderLocationInsights(filteredRows);
  renderSelectedChips();
  renderSectorButtons();
  updateFilterNote();
}

function renderStats(rows) {
  const total = rows.length;
  elements.filteredCount.textContent = total.toLocaleString();
  if (total === 0) {
    elements.filteredNote.textContent = 'No NGOs match the current combination yet.';
    elements.currentAverage.textContent = '0';
  } else {
    const average =
      rows.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.sectors.length, 0) / (rows.length || 1);
    elements.currentAverage.textContent = average.toFixed(1);
    elements.filteredNote.textContent = `${total.toLocaleString()} NGOs cover ${selectedSectors.size} selected ${
      selectedSectors.size === 1 ? 'sector' : 'sectors'
    }.`;
  }
}

function renderTopPairings(rows) {
  const counts = computeSectorCounts(rows);
  const partners = counts
    .filter((item) => !selectedSectors.has(item.name))
    .slice(0, 3);
  const fallback = counts.slice(0, 3);
  const list = partners.length ? partners : fallback;
  if (!list.length) {
    elements.pairedList.innerHTML = '<span class="pairing-item">Add filters to surface pairings.</span>';
    return;
  }
  elements.pairedList.innerHTML = list
    .map((item) => `<span class="pairing-item">${item.name} · ${item.count}</span>`)
    .join('');
}

function renderSectorChart(rows) {
  const counts = computeSectorCounts(rows).filter((item) => item.name !== DEFAULT_SECTOR);
  elements.chartCount.textContent = rows.length.toLocaleString();
  if (!counts.length) {
    elements.sectorChart.innerHTML =
      '<p class="list-message">Pick more sectors or add text to see spectrum data.</p>';
    return;
  }
  const top = counts.slice(0, 6);
  const max = Math.max(...top.map((item) => item.count), 1);
  elements.sectorChart.innerHTML = top
    .map(
      (item) => `
        <div class="sector-bar">
          <span class="sector-bar__label">${item.name}</span>
          <div class="sector-bar__track">
            <span class="sector-bar__fill" style="width:${((item.count / max) * 100).toFixed(2)}%"></span>
          </div>
          <span class="sector-bar__value">${item.count}</span>
        </div>
    `
    )
    .join('');
}

function renderList(rows) {
  const subset = rows.slice(0, LIST_LIMIT);
  if (!subset.length) {
    elements.ngoList.innerHTML =
      '<p class="list-message">No NGOs match the current stack. Try adding different sectors or text.</p>';
  } else {
    elements.ngoList.innerHTML = subset
      .map((row) => {
        const topSectors = row.sectors.slice(0, 5);
        return `
          <article class="ngo-card">
            <div>
              <h4>${row['Name of NPO'] ?? 'Unnamed NGO'}</h4>
              <p>${row.Address ?? 'Address missing'}</p>
            </div>
            <div class="badge-row">
              ${topSectors
                .map((sector) => `<span class="ngo-badge">${sector}</span>`)
                .join('')}
            </div>
            <p class="list-message">Reg: ${row['Registration No, District (State)'] ?? '—'}</p>
          </article>
        `;
      })
      .join('');
  }
  elements.listMessage.textContent = subset.length
    ? `Showing ${subset.length} of ${rows.length} NGOs that match the current filters.`
    : 'No NGOs are visible right now.';
  elements.resultCount.textContent = `${rows.length.toLocaleString()} NGOs`;
  elements.listLimit.textContent = subset.length
    ? `Showing ${subset.length}`
    : 'Showing 0';
}

function renderLocationInsights(rows) {
  const lookup = new Map();
  rows.forEach((row) => {
    const pin = extractPincode(row.Address);
    if (!pin) return;
    if (!lookup.has(pin)) {
      lookup.set(pin, []);
    }
    lookup.get(pin).push(row);
  });
  const pins = [...lookup.keys()];
  elements.locationPincodes.textContent = pins.length ? pins.length.toString() : '—';
  if (!pins.length) {
    elements.locationDistance.textContent = '—';
    elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = '<li>Pin data missing in the current slice.</li>';
    elements.locationBadge.textContent = 'Pin codes required';
    elements.locationClosest.textContent = 'Include addresses with 6-digit codes.';
    return;
  }
  if (!isPincodeMapLoaded) {
    elements.locationBadge.textContent = hasPincodeMapError
      ? 'Pin map missing'
      : 'Loading pin map…';
    elements.locationDistance.textContent = '—';
    elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = '<li>Preloaded pin map is not available yet.</li>';
    elements.locationClosest.textContent = hasPincodeMapError
      ? 'Run the fetch script to populate assets/data/pincode-locations.json.'
      : 'Asset loading in progress…';
    return;
  }
  const geocoded = pins
    .map((pin) => getLocationFromMap(pin))
    .filter(Boolean);
  if (!geocoded.length) {
    elements.locationDistance.textContent = '—';
    elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = '<li>Geocoded pincodes are not in the preloaded map.</li>';
    elements.locationBadge.textContent = 'Pin map missing entries';
    elements.locationClosest.textContent = 'Refresh the map via the helper script.';
    return;
  }
  if (geocoded.length < 2) {
    elements.locationDistance.textContent = '—';
    elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = '<li>Need at least two geocoded pincodes for distances.</li>';
    elements.locationBadge.textContent = 'Awaiting more locations';
    elements.locationClosest.textContent = 'Add NGOs with different pincodes.';
    return;
  }

  const sample = geocoded.slice(0, MAX_LOCATION_SCAN);
  const pairs = [];
  const lookupNames = new Map(lookup);
  for (let i = 0; i < sample.length; i += 1) {
    for (let j = i + 1; j < sample.length; j += 1) {
      const a = sample[i];
      const b = sample[j];
      const distance = haversine(a.latitude, a.longitude, b.latitude, b.longitude);
      pairs.push({
        distance,
        from: a,
        to: b,
      });
    }
  }
  if (!pairs.length) {
    elements.locationDistance.textContent = '—';
    elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = '<li>Not enough locations to calculate distances.</li>';
    elements.locationBadge.textContent = 'Insufficient data';
    elements.locationClosest.textContent = 'Add more NGOs.';
    return;
  }
  pairs.sort((a, b) => a.distance - b.distance);
  const averageDistance =
    pairs.reduce((sum, pair) => sum + pair.distance, 0) / pairs.length;
  elements.locationDistance.textContent = averageDistance.toFixed(1);
  const top = pairs.slice(0, 3);
  elements.locationPairs.innerHTML = top
    .map((entry) => {
      const fromNames = previewNames(entry.from.pincode, lookupNames);
      const toNames = previewNames(entry.to.pincode, lookupNames);
      return `<li>${entry.from.pincode} ↔ ${entry.to.pincode} · ${entry.distance.toFixed(
        1
      )} km • ${fromNames}${toNames ? ' / ' + toNames : ''}</li>`;
    })
    .join('');
  const closest = top[0];
  elements.locationClosest.textContent = `${closest.from.pincode} ↔ ${closest.to.pincode} ≈ ${closest.distance.toFixed(
    1
  )} km`;
  elements.locationBadge.textContent = 'Geocoded';
}

function renderSelectedChips() {
  if (!selectedSectors.size) {
    elements.selectedSectors.innerHTML =
      '<span class="pairing-item">No sectors selected yet — tap any button above.</span>';
    return;
  }
  elements.selectedSectors.innerHTML = '';
  Array.from(selectedSectors).forEach((sector) => {
    const chip = document.createElement('button');
    chip.type = 'button';
    chip.className = 'selected-chip';
    chip.innerHTML = `<span>${sector}</span><span class="remove" aria-label="Remove ${sector}">×</span>`;
    chip.addEventListener('click', () => toggleSector(sector));
    elements.selectedSectors.appendChild(chip);
  });
}

function renderSectorButtons() {
  const filter = (sectorSearchTerm ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  const list = filter
    ? datasetSectorList.filter((item) => item.name.toLowerCase().includes(filter))
    : datasetSectorList;
  elements.sectorOptions.innerHTML = '';
  if (!list.length) {
    const helper = document.createElement('p');
    helper.className = 'list-message';
    helper.textContent = 'No sectors matched that search.';
    elements.sectorOptions.appendChild(helper);
    return;
  }
  list.forEach((item) => {
    const button = document.createElement('button');
    button.type = 'button';
    button.className = 'sector-option';
    if (selectedSectors.has(item.name)) {
      button.classList.add('active');
    }
    button.innerHTML = `<span>${item.name}</span><span class="sector-count">${item.count.toLocaleString()}</span>`;
    button.addEventListener('click', () => {
      toggleSector(item.name);
    });
    elements.sectorOptions.appendChild(button);
  });
}

function toggleSector(sector) {
  if (selectedSectors.has(sector)) {
    selectedSectors.delete(sector);
  } else {
    selectedSectors.add(sector);
  }
  updateView();
}

function updateFilterNote() {
  const sectors = Array.from(selectedSectors);
  const sectorPart = sectors.length
    ? `Sectors: ${sectors.join(', ')}`
    : 'No sectors selected';
  const textPart = searchTerm ? ` · Text: “${searchTerm}”` : '';
  elements.filterNote.textContent = `${sectorPart}${textPart}`;
}

function showError(message) {
  elements.errorMessage.textContent = message;
  elements.errorMessage.style.display = 'block';
}

function previewNames(pincode, lookup) {
  const rows = lookup.get(pincode) || [];
  const names = rows
    .map((row) => row['Name of NPO'])
    .filter(Boolean)
    .slice(0, 2);
  return names.join(' / ') || 'Unnamed NGO';
}

function extractPincode(address = '') {
  const match = address.match(PINCODE_REGEX);
  return match ? match[0] : null;
}

function getLocationFromMap(pincode) {
  if (!pincode) {
    return null;
  }
  const entry = pincodeLocations?.[pincode];
  if (!entry) {
    return null;
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(entry.latitude) || !Number.isFinite(entry.longitude)) {
    return null;
  }
  return entry;
}

async function loadPincodeMap() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(PINCODE_DATA_PATH);
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
    }
    pincodeLocations = await response.json();
    isPincodeMapLoaded = true;
    hasPincodeMapError = false;
  } catch (error) {
    console.warn('Unable to load pincode map:', error);
    isPincodeMapLoaded = false;
    hasPincodeMapError = true;
  }
}

function haversine(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
  const toRad = (value) => (value * Math.PI) / 180;
  const earthRadius = 6371;
  const dLat = toRad(lat2 - lat1);
  const dLon = toRad(lon2 - lon1);
  const a =
    Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
    Math.cos(toRad(lat1)) * Math.cos(toRad(lat2)) * Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2);
  const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
  return earthRadius * c;
}

    <script>
      console.log('Collector control UI booting...');
      const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('pause-btn');
      const resumeBtn = document.getElementById('resume-btn');
      const downloadBtn = document.getElementById('download-btn');
      const statusTextEl = document.getElementById('status-text');
      const phaseLabelEl = document.getElementById('phase-label');
      const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
      const progressLabel = document.getElementById('progress-label');
      const progressCounts = document.getElementById('progress-counts');
      const recordsCollected = document.getElementById('records-collected');
      const recordsDiscovered = document.getElementById('records-discovered');
      const recordsTotal = document.getElementById('records-total');
      const recordsLimit = document.getElementById('records-limit');
      const recordsRate = document.getElementById('records-rate');
      const runtimeValue = document.getElementById('runtime-value');
      const currentRecordEl = document.getElementById('current-record');
      const lastSavedEl = document.getElementById('last-saved');
      const outputPathEl = document.getElementById('output-path');
      const logFeed = document.getElementById('log-feed');
      const logCount = document.getElementById('log-count');
      const errorsCard = document.getElementById('errors-card');
      const errorList = document.getElementById('error-list');

      const eventSource = new EventSource('/events');
      eventSource.onopen = () => {
        console.log('SSE connection established');
      };
      eventSource.onmessage = (event) => {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
        console.debug('Collector status update', data);
        renderStatus(data);
      };
      eventSource.onerror = (err) => {
        console.error('SSE connection error', err);
        statusTextEl.textContent = 'Connection interrupted. Retrying...';
      };

      pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => issueCommand('pause'));
      resumeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => issueCommand('resume'));
      downloadBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        console.log('Download requested');
        window.open('/records', '_blank');
      });

      async function issueCommand(endpoint) {
        pauseBtn.disabled = true;
        resumeBtn.disabled = true;
        try {
          await fetch(`/${endpoint}`, { method: 'POST' });
          console.log(`POST /${endpoint} succeeded`);
        } catch (err) {
          console.error('Control command failed', err);
        }
      }

      function renderStatus(data) {
        phaseLabelEl.textContent = sentenceCase(data.phase || 'unknown');
        statusTextEl.textContent = data.lastMessage || 'Standing by.';
        recordsCollected.textContent = formatNumber(data.processedRecords || 0);
        recordsDiscovered.textContent = formatNumber(data.discoveredRows || 0);
        recordsTotal.textContent = data.totalRows ? formatNumber(data.totalRows) : '--';
        recordsLimit.textContent = data.maxRecords ? formatNumber(data.maxRecords) : 'none';
        recordsRate.textContent = (data.recordsPerMinute || 0).toFixed(2);
        runtimeValue.textContent = formatDuration(data.runtimeMs || 0);
        currentRecordEl.textContent = data.currentRecord || '--';
        lastSavedEl.textContent = data.lastSavedAt ? formatTime(data.lastSavedAt) : '--';
        outputPathEl.textContent = data.outputPath || 'n/a';

        const progressMax =
          data.totalRows ||
          data.maxRecords ||
          data.discoveredRows ||
          data.processedRecords ||
          1;
        const progressCurrent = Math.min(data.processedRecords || 0, progressMax);
        const percent = Math.min(100, (progressCurrent / progressMax) * 100);
        progressFill.style.width = `${percent.toFixed(1)}%`;
        progressLabel.textContent = `${percent.toFixed(1)}%`;
        progressCounts.textContent = `${formatNumber(progressCurrent)} / ${
          progressMax ? formatNumber(progressMax) : '?'
        } records`;

        const logs = (data.logs || []).slice(-40).reverse();
        logFeed.innerHTML = logs
          .map(
            (log) =>
              `<li><span>[${formatTime(log.ts)}]</span>${escapeHtml(log.message || '')}</li>`
          )
          .join('');
        logCount.textContent = `${logs.length} entr${logs.length === 1 ? 'y' : 'ies'}`;

        if (data.errors && data.errors.length) {
          errorsCard.hidden = false;
          errorList.innerHTML = data.errors
            .slice(-10)
            .map(
              (err) =>
                `<li><strong>${formatTime(err.ts || '')}:</strong> ${escapeHtml(
                  err.message || String(err)
                )}</li>`
            )
            .join('');
        } else {
          errorsCard.hidden = true;
          errorList.innerHTML = '';
        }

        const isTerminal = ['completed', 'error'].includes((data.phase || '').toLowerCase());
        pauseBtn.disabled = data.paused || isTerminal;
        resumeBtn.disabled = !data.paused || isTerminal;
        downloadBtn.disabled = !(data.processedRecords || 0) && !isTerminal;
      }

      function formatNumber(value) {
        return new Intl.NumberFormat().format(value || 0);
      }

      function formatDuration(ms) {
        if (!ms) return '0s';
        const seconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
        if (seconds < 60) {
          return `${seconds}s`;
        }
        const minutes = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
        const remaining = seconds % 60;
        if (minutes < 60) {
          return `${minutes}m ${remaining}s`;
        }
        const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
        const remMinutes = minutes % 60;
        return `${hours}h ${remMinutes}m`;
      }

      function formatTime(value) {
        if (!value) return '--:--:--';
        const date = new Date(value);
        return date.toLocaleTimeString();
      }

      function escapeHtml(text) {
        return String(text || '')
          .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
          .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
          .replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
      }

      function sentenceCase(value) {
        if (!value) return 'Unknown';
        const lower = value.toLowerCase();
        return lower.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lower.slice(1);
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

================
File: scripts/fetch-pincode-locations.js
================
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const OUTPUT_FILE = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'assets', 'data', 'pincode-locations.json');
const TABLE_FILE = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'outputs', 'table-results.json');
const API_BASE = 'https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org/search';
const DELAY_MS = 1300;

function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

function extractPincode(address = '') {
  const match = address.match(/\b\d{6}\b/);
  return match ? match[0] : null;
}

async function fetchPincode(pin) {
  const url = `${API_BASE}?postalcode=${encodeURIComponent(pin)}&country=India&format=json&limit=1`;
  const response = await fetch(url, {
    headers: {
      'User-Agent': 'NGO-dashboard/1.0 (admin@example.com)',
    },
  });
  if (!response.ok) {
    throw new Error(`${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);
  }
  const results = await response.json();
  if (!Array.isArray(results) || !results.length) {
    return null;
  }
  const [record] = results;
  const latitude = Number(record.lat);
  const longitude = Number(record.lon);
  if (!Number.isFinite(latitude) || !Number.isFinite(longitude)) {
    return null;
  }
  return {
    pincode: pin,
    latitude,
    longitude,
    display: record.display_name,
  };
}

async function main() {
  if (!fs.existsSync(TABLE_FILE)) {
    console.error('Missing table data; run the scraper first.');
    process.exit(1);
  }
  const tableData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(TABLE_FILE, 'utf8'));
  const rows = Array.isArray(tableData.table?.rows) ? tableData.table.rows : [];
  const pins = new Set();
  rows.forEach((row) => {
    const pin = extractPincode(row.Address);
    if (pin) {
      pins.add(pin);
    }
  });

  if (!pins.size) {
    console.log('No pincodes detected in the dataset.');
    return;
  }

  const existing = fs.existsSync(OUTPUT_FILE)
    ? JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(OUTPUT_FILE, 'utf8'))
    : {};

  const queue = [...pins].filter(
    (pin) =>
      !Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(existing, pin) || existing[pin] === null
  );
  if (!queue.length) {
    console.log('All pincodes already resolved.');
    return;
  }

  console.log(`Resolving ${queue.length} new pincodes…`);
  for (const pin of queue) {
    try {
      const location = await fetchPincode(pin);
      existing[pin] = location;
      fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(OUTPUT_FILE), { recursive: true });
      fs.writeFileSync(OUTPUT_FILE, JSON.stringify(existing, null, 2));
      console.log(`Saved ${pin}: ${location ? 'geocoded' : 'no result'}`);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Failed to fetch ${pin}:`, error.message);
      existing[pin] = null;
    }
    await sleep(DELAY_MS);
  }
  console.log('Pincode refresh complete.');
}

main().catch((error) => {
  console.error('Unable to build pincode map:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});

================
File: scripts/record-workflow.js
================
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { chromium } = require('playwright');

const OUTPUT_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'outputs');
const TRACE_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'workflow.trace.zip');

async function ensureOutputDir() {
  fs.mkdirSync(OUTPUT_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

async function run() {
  await ensureOutputDir();
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: false });
  const context = await browser.newContext();
  const page = await context.newPage();

  console.log('Starting tracing session. Interact with the browser if needed.');
  await context.tracing.start({
    screenshots: true,
    snapshots: true,
  });

  await page.goto('https://ngodarpan.gov.in/#/search-ngo', {
    waitUntil: 'networkidle',
    timeout: 60000,
  });

  console.log('Page loaded. Tracing will record for 45 seconds before stopping.');
  await page.waitForTimeout(45000);

  await context.tracing.stop({ path: TRACE_PATH });
  console.log(`Tracing stopped and saved to ${TRACE_PATH}.`);

  await browser.close();
}

run().catch((err) => {
  console.error('Recording failed:', err);
  process.exit(1);
});

================
File: scripts/collect-detailed-data.js

require('dotenv').config();
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const http = require('http');
const { webkit } = require('playwright');

const OUTPUT_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'outputs');
const DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'optimized-detail-records.json');
const CONTROL_UI_PATH = path.join(process.cwd(), 'collector.html');
const SERVER_PORT = Number(process.env.COLLECTOR_PORT || process.env.SCRAPER_PORT || 4173);
const HEADLESS = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_HEADLESS !== 'false';
const MAX_RECORDS = Number.isFinite(Number(process.env.MAX_DETAIL_RECORDS))
  ? Number(process.env.MAX_DETAIL_RECORDS)
  : null;
const LOG_LIMIT = 200;

const PREFERRED_MODEL = 'gpt-5.1-nano';
const FALLBACK_MODEL = 'gpt-4o-mini';
const CAPTCHA_PROMPT = [
  'You are a captcha reader. Output only the characters shown in the attached image.',
  'Do not add any commentary, punctuation, whitespace, or labels - only the captcha characters.',
  'If the image is unclear, respond with the characters you can confidently see.',
].join(' ');

const OPENAI_API_KEY = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY || '';

const SELECTIONS = {
  selectedState: 'Karnataka',
  selectedDistrict: 'BENGALURU URBAN',
  selectedSectors: ['Differently Abled'],
  selectedNgoTypes: ['Section 8 Company', 'Society', 'Trust'],
};

const DATE_SELECTOR =
  '#commonScrollTo > div.masonry-container.ng-star-inserted > p-card:nth-child(2) > div > div > div.p-card-content > div > div:nth-child(7) > p';
const EMAIL_SECTION_SELECTOR =
  '#commonScrollTo > div.masonry-container.ng-star-inserted > p-card:nth-child(4) > div > div > div.p-card-content > div > div:nth-child(2) > p';
const EMAIL_VIEW_TEXT = 'View NPO Email';
const EMAIL_LABEL_TEXT = 'NPO Contact Email';

const state = {
  phase: 'booting',
  paused: false,
  startedAt: null,
  finishedAt: null,
  processedRecords: 0,
  discoveredRows: 0,
  totalRows: null,
  totalPages: null,
  rowsPerPage: null,
  currentPage: 0,
  rowsInCurrentPage: 0,
  currentRecord: null,
  lastMessage: 'Preparing collector',
  lastSavedAt: null,
  durationMs: null,
  controlUrl: null,
  errors: [],
  logs: [],
  outputPath: DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH,
  selections: SELECTIONS,
};

const sseClients = new Set();
const pauseController = { paused: false, previousPhase: null };
let controlServer = null;

function delay(ms) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

function updateState(patch = {}) {
  Object.assign(state, patch);
  broadcast();
}

function log(message, level = 'info') {
  const entry = { ts: new Date().toISOString(), level, message };
  state.logs.push(entry);
  if (state.logs.length > LOG_LIMIT) {
    state.logs.shift();
  }
  const consoleMethod = level === 'error' ? console.error : console.log;
  consoleMethod(`[collector] ${message}`);
  broadcast();
}

function addError(message) {
  state.errors.push({ ts: new Date().toISOString(), message });
  if (state.errors.length > 25) {
    state.errors.shift();
  }
}

function buildStatus() {
  const runtimeMs =
    state.startedAt && (state.finishedAt || state.phase)
      ? (state.finishedAt
          ? new Date(state.finishedAt).getTime()
          : Date.now()) - new Date(state.startedAt).getTime()
      : 0;
  const recordsPerMinute =
    runtimeMs > 0 ? Number((state.processedRecords / (runtimeMs / 60000)).toFixed(2)) : 0;
  return {
    ...state,
    runtimeMs,
    recordsPerMinute,
    serverPort: SERVER_PORT,
    maxRecords: MAX_RECORDS,
  };
}

function broadcast() {
  if (!sseClients.size) {
    return;
  }
  const payload = `data: ${JSON.stringify(buildStatus())}\n\n`;
  for (const client of Array.from(sseClients)) {
    try {
      client.write(payload);
    } catch (err) {
      sseClients.delete(client);
      console.error('[collector] SSE client disconnected:', err.message);
    }
  }
}

async function ensureOutputDir() {
  fs.mkdirSync(OUTPUT_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

function requestPause(origin = 'operator') {
  if (pauseController.paused) {
    return;
  }
  pauseController.paused = true;
  pauseController.previousPhase = state.phase;
  updateState({ paused: true, phase: 'paused', lastMessage: `Paused by ${origin}` });
  log(`Paused collection (${origin})`);
}

function requestResume(origin = 'operator') {
  if (!pauseController.paused) {
    return;
  }
  pauseController.paused = false;
  const restoredPhase = pauseController.previousPhase || 'collecting';
  pauseController.previousPhase = null;
  updateState({ paused: false, phase: restoredPhase, lastMessage: `Resumed by ${origin}` });
  log(`Resumed collection (${origin})`);
}

async function waitWhilePaused(label = 'continuing') {
  while (pauseController.paused) {
    updateState({ lastMessage: `Paused before ${label}` });
    await delay(250);
  }
}

function serveControlUi(res) {
  try {
    const html = fs.readFileSync(CONTROL_UI_PATH, 'utf8');
    res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'text/html; charset=utf-8' });
    res.end(html);
  } catch (err) {
    res.writeHead(500, { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain; charset=utf-8' });
    res.end(`Control UI not found at ${CONTROL_UI_PATH}: ${err.message}`);
  }
}

function serveRecords(res) {
  if (!fs.existsSync(DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH)) {
    res.writeHead(404, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
    res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Output not ready yet.' }));
    return;
  }
  res.writeHead(200, {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
  });
  fs.createReadStream(DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH).pipe(res);
}

function attachEventStream(req, res) {
  res.writeHead(200, {
    'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
    'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
    Connection: 'keep-alive',
  });
  res.write(`data: ${JSON.stringify(buildStatus())}\n\n`);
  const clientId = `${req.socket.remoteAddress || 'unknown'}:${req.socket.remotePort || '0'}`;
  log(`SSE client connected (${clientId})`);
  sseClients.add(res);
  req.on('close', () => {
    sseClients.delete(res);
    log(`SSE client disconnected (${clientId})`);
  });
}

async function startControlServer() {
  if (controlServer) {
    return controlServer;
  }
  controlServer = http.createServer((req, res) => {
    const parsed = new URL(req.url, `http://${req.headers.host}`);
    const { pathname } = parsed;
    log(`HTTP ${req.method} ${pathname}`);

    if (req.method === 'GET' && pathname === '/') {
      return serveControlUi(res);
    }
    if (req.method === 'GET' && pathname === '/status') {
      res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
      res.end(JSON.stringify(buildStatus()));
      return;
    }
    if (req.method === 'GET' && pathname === '/events') {
      return attachEventStream(req, res);
    }
    if (req.method === 'GET' && pathname === '/records') {
      log('UI requested latest records download');
      return serveRecords(res);
    }
    if (req.method === 'POST' && pathname === '/pause') {
      requestPause('UI');
      log('Pause endpoint invoked by UI');
      res.writeHead(204).end();
      return;
    }
    if (req.method === 'POST' && pathname === '/resume') {
      requestResume('UI');
      log('Resume endpoint invoked by UI');
      res.writeHead(204).end();
      return;
    }

    res.writeHead(404, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
    res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Not found' }));
  });

  await new Promise((resolve) => {
    controlServer.listen(SERVER_PORT, () => {
      const url = `http://localhost:${SERVER_PORT}/`;
      updateState({ controlUrl: url });
      log(`Collector control UI ready at ${url}`);
      resolve();
    });
  });

  return controlServer;
}

async function selectDropdownOption(page, formControlName, optionText) {
  const dropdown = page.locator(`p-dropdown[formcontrolname="${formControlName}"]`);
  await dropdown.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  await dropdown.locator('.p-dropdown-trigger').click();
  const option = page.locator('.p-dropdown-items li', { hasText: optionText }).first();
  await option.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  await option.click();
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);
}

async function selectMultiOptions(page, formControlName, optionTexts) {
  const multiselect = page.locator(`p-multiselect[formcontrolname="${formControlName}"]`);
  await multiselect.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  await multiselect.locator('.p-multiselect-label-container').click();
  await page.waitForSelector('.p-multiselect-panel:visible', { timeout: 20000 });
  const panel = page.locator('.p-multiselect-panel:visible').first();
  for (const text of optionTexts) {
    const item = panel.locator('.p-multiselect-item', { hasText: text }).first();
    await item.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
    await item.click();
    await page.waitForTimeout(250);
  }
  await page.keyboard.press('Escape');
}

async function waitForSearchButtonEnabled(page) {
  const context = { selector: '#commonScrollTo button', text: 'Search' };
  await page.waitForFunction(
    ({ selector, text }) => {
      const buttons = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
      const target = buttons.find((button) => button.textContent.trim() === text);
      return !!target && !target.disabled;
    },
    context,
    { timeout: 60000 }
  );
  return page.locator('#commonScrollTo button', { hasText: 'Search' }).first();
}

async function captureCaptcha(page) {
  const captchaCanvas = page.locator('canvas.captcha-canvas');
  await captchaCanvas.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  const buffer = await captchaCanvas.screenshot();
  return buffer.toString('base64');
}

async function decodeCaptchaText(imageBase64) {
  if (!OPENAI_API_KEY) {
    throw new Error('Set OPENAI_API_KEY before running this script so we can decode the captcha.');
  }

  const buildBody = (model) => ({
    model,
    input: [
      {
        role: 'user',
        content: [
          { type: 'input_text', text: CAPTCHA_PROMPT },
          { type: 'input_image', image_url: `data:image/png;base64,${imageBase64}` },
        ],
      },
    ],
  });

  const callModel = async (model) => {
    const response = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/responses', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        Authorization: `Bearer ${OPENAI_API_KEY}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(buildBody(model)),
    });

    const raw = await response.text();
    if (!response.ok) {
      const err = new Error(`OpenAI responded with ${response.status}: ${raw}`);
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
        if (parsed?.error?.code) {
          err.code = parsed.error.code;
        }
      } catch {
        // ignore JSON parsing failures
      }
      throw err;
    }

    const payload = JSON.parse(raw);
    const text = extractTextFromOpenAIResponse(payload);
    if (!text) {
      throw new Error('Unable to determine captcha text from OpenAI response.');
    }
    return text;
  };

  try {
    return await callModel(PREFERRED_MODEL);
  } catch (err) {
    if (err.code === 'model_not_found') {
      log(`Model ${PREFERRED_MODEL} unavailable; falling back to ${FALLBACK_MODEL}.`, 'error');
      return callModel(FALLBACK_MODEL);
    }
    throw err;
  }
}

function extractTextFromOpenAIResponse(payload) {
  if (!payload) return null;
  if (typeof payload.output_text === 'string' && payload.output_text.trim()) {
    return payload.output_text.trim();
  }

  const outputs = Array.isArray(payload.output) ? payload.output : [];
  const pieces = [];
  for (const output of outputs) {
    if (typeof output?.content === 'string') {
      pieces.push(output.content.trim());
      continue;
    }
    const content = Array.isArray(output?.content) ? output.content : [];
    for (const block of content) {
      if (block?.type === 'output_text' && typeof block.text === 'string') {
        pieces.push(block.text.trim());
      }
    }
  }

  return pieces.filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim();
}

async function extractTable(page) {
  await page.waitForSelector('table tbody tr', { timeout: 60000 });
  return page.$eval('table', (table) => {
    const headerNodes = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('thead th'));
    const headers =
      headerNodes.length > 0
        ? headerNodes.map((node) => node.textContent.trim() || null)
        : [];
    const rows = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr')).map((tr) => {
      const cells = Array.from(tr.querySelectorAll('td'));
      const rowObj = {};
      cells.forEach((cell, index) => {
        const key = headers?.[index] || `column${index + 1}`;
        rowObj[key] = cell.textContent.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
      });
      return rowObj;
    });
    return { headers, rows };
  });
}

async function readTotalRowsFromPaginator(page) {
  const summaryLocator = page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom .p-paginator-current');
  if ((await summaryLocator.count()) === 0) {
    return null;
  }
  const text = await summaryLocator.textContent();
  if (!text) return null;
  const match = text.replace(/,/g, '').match(/of\s+(\d+)/i);
  return match ? Number(match[1]) : null;
}

async function goToNextPage(page) {
  const paginator = page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom .p-paginator-next').first();
  if ((await paginator.count()) === 0) {
    return false;
  }
  const disabled = await paginator.evaluate(
    (btn) => btn.disabled || btn.classList.contains('p-disabled')
  );
  if (disabled) {
    return false;
  }

  const previousSignature = await page
    .locator('table tbody tr td:first-child')
    .first()
    .textContent()
    .catch(() => null);

  await paginator.click();
  await page
    .waitForFunction(
      (signature) => {
        const firstCell = document.querySelector('table tbody tr td');
        if (!firstCell) return false;
        const current = firstCell.textContent?.trim() || '';
        return current !== (signature || '').trim();
      },
      previousSignature || '',
      { timeout: 20000 }
    )
    .catch(() => delay(1200));
  await page.waitForTimeout(500);
  return true;
}

function normalizeRow(row) {
  const serial = row['Sr. No.'] || row['Sr No.'] || row['Sr. No'] || row['Sr No'] || null;
  const name =
    row['Name of NPO'] ||
    row['Name of NGO'] ||
    row['Name'] ||
    row['Ngo Name'] ||
    row['NPO Name'] ||
    null;
  const registrationRaw =
    row['Registration No, District (State)'] ||
    row['Registration No'] ||
    row['Registration Number'] ||
    null;
  const address = row['Address'] || row['Address / Location'] || row.address || null;
  const sectorsRaw =
    row['Sectors working in'] ||
    row['Sectors'] ||
    row['Sector'] ||
    row['Sectors Working'] ||
    '';
  const sectors = sectorsRaw
    .split(',')
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
  const registration = parseRegistrationInfo(registrationRaw);

  return {
    serialNumber: typeof serial === 'string' ? Number(serial) || serial : serial,
    name,
    address,
    sectors,
    registration,
    raw: row,
  };
}

function parseRegistrationInfo(raw) {
  if (!raw) {
    return {
      raw: null,
      number: null,
      district: null,
      state: null,
    };
  }
  const cleaned = raw.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
  const pattern = /^(.*?)\s+([^()]+?)\s+\(([^()]+)\)$/;
  const match = cleaned.match(pattern);
  if (!match) {
    return {
      raw: cleaned,
      number: cleaned,
      district: null,
      state: null,
    };
  }
  const [, numberPart, districtPart, statePart] = match;
  return {
    raw: cleaned,
    number: numberPart.trim(),
    district: districtPart.trim(),
    state: statePart.trim(),
  };
}

async function gatherDetailForRow(page, rowIndex) {
  await waitWhilePaused(`opening row ${rowIndex + 1}`);
  const rowLocator = page.locator('table tbody tr').nth(rowIndex);
  await rowLocator.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 60000 });
  const nameLink = rowLocator.locator('td:nth-child(2) a').first();
  await nameLink.scrollIntoViewIfNeeded();
  await nameLink.click();
  let detailMode = false;
  try {
    await page.waitForSelector(DATE_SELECTOR, { timeout: 45000 });
    detailMode = true;
    const dateText = await page.locator(DATE_SELECTOR).textContent();
    const dateOfRegistration = extractDate(dateText);

    const emailSection = page.locator(EMAIL_SECTION_SELECTOR);
    await emailSection.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
    const viewLink = emailSection.locator('a', { hasText: EMAIL_VIEW_TEXT }).first();
    if ((await viewLink.count()) > 0) {
      await viewLink.click();
    }

    await emailSection.locator('span', { hasText: EMAIL_LABEL_TEXT }).waitFor({ timeout: 15000 });
    const emailText = await emailSection.evaluate((node) => {
      const label = node.querySelector('span')?.textContent || '';
      let text = node.textContent || '';
      if (label) {
        text = text.replace(label, '');
      }
      return text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
    });

    const normalizedEmail = normalizeEmail(emailText);
    return {
      dateOfRegistration,
      email: normalizedEmail,
    };
  } finally {
    if (detailMode) {
      await clickBackToTable(page);
    }
  }
}

function extractDate(text) {
  if (!text) return null;
  const trimmed = text.trim();
  const match = trimmed.match(/\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}/);
  return match ? match[0] : trimmed;
}

function normalizeEmail(value) {
  return (
    value
      ?.replace(/\[at\]/gi, '@')
      .replace(/\[dot\]/gi, '.')
      .replace(/\s+/g, '')
      .trim() || null
  );
}

async function clickBackToTable(page) {
  const backButton = page.locator('#exclude > p-button:nth-child(2) > button');
  await backButton.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 30000 });
  await backButton.click();
  await page.waitForSelector('table tbody tr', { timeout: 60000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(400);
}

function createRecordWriter(meta) {
  const stream = fs.createWriteStream(meta.path);
  let closed = false;
  let isFirst = true;
  const capturedAt = new Date().toISOString();

  stream.on('error', (err) => {
    log(`Writer stream error: ${err.message}`, 'error');
  });

  stream.write('{\n');
  stream.write(`  "capturedAt": ${JSON.stringify(capturedAt)},\n`);
  stream.write(
    `  "selections": ${JSON.stringify(meta.selections, null, 2).replace(/\n/g, '\n  ')},\n`
  );
  stream.write(
    `  "tableHeaders": ${JSON.stringify(meta.headers || [], null, 2).replace(/\n/g, '\n  ')},\n`
  );
  stream.write('  "records": [');

  return {
    write(record) {
      if (closed) {
        throw new Error('Cannot write to closed stream.');
      }
      const payload = JSON.stringify(record);
      stream.write(isFirst ? `\n    ${payload}` : `,\n    ${payload}`);
      isFirst = false;
    },
    finalize(stats) {
      if (closed) {
        return;
      }
      stream.write('\n  ],\n');
      stream.write(`  "stats": ${JSON.stringify(stats, null, 2).replace(/\n/g, '\n  ')}\n`);
      stream.write('}\n');
      stream.end();
      closed = true;
    },
  };
}

async function processPageRows(page, pageData, pageIndex, writer) {
  state.rowsPerPage = state.rowsPerPage || pageData.rows.length || null;
  state.currentPage = pageIndex;
  state.rowsInCurrentPage = pageData.rows.length;
  state.discoveredRows += pageData.rows.length;
  updateState({
    phase: 'collecting',
    currentPage: pageIndex,
    rowsInCurrentPage: pageData.rows.length,
    discoveredRows: state.discoveredRows,
  });

  for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < pageData.rows.length; rowIndex += 1) {
    await waitWhilePaused(`row ${rowIndex + 1} on page ${pageIndex}`);
    const summary = normalizeRow(pageData.rows[rowIndex]);
    state.currentRecord = summary.name || summary.registration?.number || `row-${rowIndex + 1}`;
    updateState({ currentRecord: state.currentRecord });

    let detail;
    try {
      detail = await gatherDetailForRow(page, rowIndex);
    } catch (err) {
      const message = `Failed to capture detail for ${state.currentRecord}: ${err.message}`;
      log(message, 'error');
      addError(message);
      detail = { error: err.message };
    }

    writer.write({
      index: state.processedRecords + 1,
      collectedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      page: pageIndex,
      rowInPage: rowIndex + 1,
      summary,
      detail,
    });

    state.processedRecords += 1;
    state.lastSavedAt = new Date().toISOString();
    updateState({
      processedRecords: state.processedRecords,
      lastSavedAt: state.lastSavedAt,
      lastMessage: `Captured ${state.processedRecords} record(s)`,
    });

    if (MAX_RECORDS && state.processedRecords >= MAX_RECORDS) {
      log(`MAX_RECORDS=${MAX_RECORDS} reached. Stopping collection.`, 'info');
      return 'stop';
    }
  }

  return 'continue';
}

async function collectAcrossPages(page, writer, firstPageData) {
  let pageIndex = 1;
  let currentPageData = firstPageData;

  while (true) {
    const status = await processPageRows(page, currentPageData, pageIndex, writer);
    if (status === 'stop') {
      return;
    }

    const hasNext = await goToNextPage(page);
    if (!hasNext) {
      return;
    }

    pageIndex += 1;
    currentPageData = await extractTable(page);
  }
}

function buildFinalStats(durationMs, status) {
  return {
    durationMs,
    status,
    processedRecords: state.processedRecords,
    discoveredRows: state.discoveredRows,
    reportedTotalRows: state.totalRows,
    totalPages: state.totalPages,
    limitApplied: Boolean(MAX_RECORDS && state.processedRecords >= MAX_RECORDS),
    errors: state.errors,
  };
}

async function runCollector() {
  await ensureOutputDir();
  await startControlServer();

  const startTime = Date.now();
  updateState({ phase: 'launching-browser', startedAt: new Date().toISOString() });

  const browser = await webkit.launch({ headless: HEADLESS });
  const page = await browser.newPage();
  let writer = null;

  try {
    log('Navigating to NGO Darpan search page...');
    await page.goto('https://ngodarpan.gov.in/#/search-ngo', {
      waitUntil: 'networkidle',
      timeout: 60000,
    });

    updateState({ phase: 'configuring-search', lastMessage: 'Applying filters' });
    await selectDropdownOption(page, 'selectedState', SELECTIONS.selectedState);
    await page.waitForTimeout(800);
    await selectDropdownOption(page, 'selectedDistrict', SELECTIONS.selectedDistrict);
    await selectMultiOptions(page, 'selectedSectors', SELECTIONS.selectedSectors);
    await selectMultiOptions(page, 'selectedNgoTypes', SELECTIONS.selectedNgoTypes);

    updateState({ phase: 'solving-captcha', lastMessage: 'Decoding captcha' });
    const captchaImageBase64 = await captureCaptcha(page);
    const captchaText = await decodeCaptchaText(captchaImageBase64);
    log(`Decoded captcha text: ${captchaText}`);
    await page.fill('#captchaInput', captchaText);

    const searchButton = await waitForSearchButtonEnabled(page);
    await searchButton.click();
    log('Search submitted. Waiting for table results...');

    await page.waitForTimeout(4000);
    await page.waitForSelector('table tbody tr', { timeout: 60000 });

    const totalRows = await readTotalRowsFromPaginator(page);
    const firstPageData = await extractTable(page);
    const rowsPerPage = firstPageData.rows.length || null;
    const totalPages =
      totalRows && rowsPerPage ? Math.ceil(totalRows / rowsPerPage) : null;

    updateState({
      phase: 'collecting',
      totalRows,
      totalPages,
      rowsPerPage,
      discoveredRows: 0,
      lastMessage: 'Starting detailed capture',
    });

    writer = createRecordWriter({
      path: DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH,
      selections: SELECTIONS,
      headers: firstPageData.headers,
    });

    await collectAcrossPages(page, writer, firstPageData);

    const finalStats = buildFinalStats(Date.now() - startTime, 'completed');
    writer.finalize(finalStats);
    updateState({
      phase: 'completed',
      finishedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      durationMs: finalStats.durationMs,
      lastMessage: 'Collection completed',
    });
    log(`Collection complete. ${state.processedRecords} record(s) written to ${DETAIL_OUTPUT_PATH}.`);
  } catch (err) {
    const finalStats = buildFinalStats(Date.now() - startTime, 'error');
    if (writer) {
      writer.finalize(finalStats);
    }
    addError(err.message);
    updateState({
      phase: 'error',
      finishedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      durationMs: finalStats.durationMs,
      lastMessage: `Search workflow failed: ${err.message}`,
    });
    log(`Search workflow failed: ${err.stack || err.message}`, 'error');
    throw err;
  } finally {
    await browser.close().catch(() => {});
  }
}

function handleShutdown(signal) {
  log(`Received ${signal}. Shutting down...`);
  requestPause('shutdown');
  if (controlServer) {
    controlServer.close();
  }
  process.exit(0);
}

process.on('SIGINT', () => handleShutdown('SIGINT'));
process.on('SIGTERM', () => handleShutdown('SIGTERM'));

runCollector().catch((err) => {
  console.error('Collector failed:', err);
  process.exit(1);
});

const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { webkit } = require('playwright');

const OUTPUT_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), 'outputs');
const CAPTCHA_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'captcha.png');
const TABLE_DATA_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'table-results.json');
const TABLE_SCREENSHOT_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'table.png');
const DETAILED_RECORD_PATH = path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'detailed-record.json');
const DATE_SECTION_SELECTOR =
  '#commonScrollTo > div.masonry-container.ng-star-inserted > p-card:nth-child(2) > div > div > div.p-card-content > div > div:nth-child(7) > p';
const EMAIL_SECTION_SELECTOR =
  '#commonScrollTo > div.masonry-container.ng-star-inserted > p-card:nth-child(4) > div > div > div.p-card-content > div > div:nth-child(2) > p';
const EMAIL_VIEW_LINK_TEXT = 'View NPO Email';
const EMAIL_LABEL_TEXT = 'NPO Contact Email';

const OPENAI_API_KEY = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY || '';

const SELECTIONS = {
  selectedState: 'Karnataka',
  selectedDistrict: 'BENGALURU URBAN',
  selectedSectors: ['Differently Abled'],
  selectedNgoTypes: ['Section 8 Company', 'Society', 'Trust'],
};

  fs.mkdirSync(OUTPUT_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

}

  await multiselect.locator('.p-multiselect-label-container').click();

}

  await page.waitForFunction(
    ({ selector, text }) => {
      const buttons = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
      const target = buttons.find((button) => button.textContent.trim() === text);
      return !!target && !target.disabled;
    },
    context,
    { timeout: 60000 }
  );
  return page.locator('#commonScrollTo button', { hasText: 'Search' }).first();
}

async function captureCaptcha(page) {
  const captchaCanvas = page.locator('canvas.captcha-canvas');
  await captchaCanvas.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  await captchaCanvas.screenshot({ path: CAPTCHA_PATH });
  const imageBase64 = fs.readFileSync(CAPTCHA_PATH, { encoding: 'base64' });
  return imageBase64;
}

async function decodeCaptchaText(imageBase64) {
  const apiKey = OPENAI_API_KEY;
  if (!apiKey) {
    throw new Error(
      'Set OPENAI_API_KEY before running this script so we can decode the captcha.'
    );
  }

  const body = {
    model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
    input: [
      {
        role: 'user',
        content: [
          {
            type: 'input_text',
            text: 'Extract the text shown in the attached captcha image. Reply with the characters only.',
          },
          {
            type: 'input_image',
            image_url: `data:image/png;base64,${imageBase64}`,
          },
        ],
      },
    ],
  };

  const response = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/responses', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const text = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`OpenAI responded with ${response.status}: ${text}`);
  }

  const payload = await response.json();
  const text = extractTextFromOpenAIResponse(payload);
  if (!text) {
    throw new Error('Unable to determine captcha text from OpenAI response.');
  }
  return text;
}

function extractTextFromOpenAIResponse(payload) {
  if (!payload) return null;
  if (typeof payload.output_text === 'string' && payload.output_text.trim()) {
    return payload.output_text.trim();
  }

  const outputs = Array.isArray(payload.output) ? payload.output : [];
  const pieces = [];
  for (const output of outputs) {
    if (typeof output?.content === 'string') {
      pieces.push(output.content.trim());
      continue;
    }
    const content = Array.isArray(output?.content) ? output.content : [];
    for (const block of content) {
      if (block?.type === 'output_text' && typeof block.text === 'string') {
        pieces.push(block.text.trim());
      }
    }
  }

  return pieces.filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim();
}

async function extractTable(page) {
  await page.waitForSelector('table', { timeout: 60000 });
  return page.$eval('table', (table) => {
    const headerNodes = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('thead th'));
    const headers =
      headerNodes.length > 0
        ? headerNodes.map((node) => node.textContent.trim() || null)
        : null;
    const rows = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr')).map((tr) => {
      const cells = Array.from(tr.querySelectorAll('td'));
      const rowObj = {};
      cells.forEach((cell, index) => {
        const key =
          headers?.[index] ||
          `column${index + 1}` ||
          `column${index + 1}`;
        rowObj[key] = cell.textContent.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
      });
      return rowObj;
    });
    return {
      headers: headers ?? [],
      rowCount: rows.length,
      rows,
    };
  });
}

async function collectAllTableRows(page) {
  const aggregatedRows = [];
  let headers = null;
  await page.waitForSelector('.p-paginator-bottom', { timeout: 20000 });
  while (true) {
    const tableData = await extractTable(page);
    if (!headers) {
      headers = tableData.headers;
    }
    aggregatedRows.push(...tableData.rows);

    if ((await page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom').count()) === 0) {
      break;
    }
    const nextButton = page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom .p-paginator-next').first();
    await nextButton.waitFor({ state: 'attached', timeout: 10000 });
    const nextDisabled = await nextButton.evaluate(
      (btn) => btn.disabled || btn.classList.contains('p-disabled')
    );
    if (nextDisabled) {
      break;
    }

    const currentButton = page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom .p-paginator-pages button[aria-current="page"]');
    const currentLabel = await currentButton.getAttribute('aria-label');
    const currentPageNumber = Number.parseInt(currentLabel ?? '1', 10) || 1;
    const nextLabel = `${currentPageNumber + 1}`;

    await nextButton.click();
    await page.waitForFunction(
      (label) => {
        const current = document.querySelector('.p-paginator-pages button[aria-current="page"]');
        return current?.getAttribute('aria-label') === label;
      },
      nextLabel
    );
    await page.waitForTimeout(1000);
  }

  return {
    headers: headers ?? [],
    rows: aggregatedRows,
  };
}

async function ensureFirstPageDisplayed(page) {
  const firstPageButton = page.locator('.p-paginator-bottom .p-paginator-first').first();
  if ((await firstPageButton.count()) === 0) {
    return;
  }

  const isDisabled = await firstPageButton.evaluate(
    (button) => button.disabled || button.classList.contains('p-disabled')
  );
  if (isDisabled) {
    return;
  }

  await firstPageButton.click();
  await page.waitForFunction(
    () => {
      const current = document.querySelector('.p-paginator-pages button[aria-current="page"]');
      return current?.getAttribute('aria-label') === 'Page 1';
    },
    undefined,
    { timeout: 20000 }
  );
  await page.waitForTimeout(800);
}

async function captureDetailForFirstRecord(page) {
  const firstRecordLink = page.locator('table tbody tr').first().locator('td a').first();
  await firstRecordLink.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  await firstRecordLink.click();

  await page.waitForSelector(DATE_SECTION_SELECTOR, { timeout: 30000 });
  const dateText = await page.locator(DATE_SECTION_SELECTOR).textContent();

  const emailSection = page.locator(EMAIL_SECTION_SELECTOR);
  await emailSection.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 20000 });
  const viewLink = emailSection.locator('a', { hasText: EMAIL_VIEW_LINK_TEXT }).first();
  if ((await viewLink.count()) > 0) {
    await viewLink.click();
  }

  await emailSection
    .locator('span', { hasText: EMAIL_LABEL_TEXT })
    .waitFor({ timeout: 15000 });

  const emailText = await emailSection.evaluate((node) => {
    const label = node.querySelector('span')?.textContent || '';
    let text = node.textContent || '';
    if (label) {
      text = text.replace(label, '');
    }
    return text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
  });

  return {
    dateOfRegistration: dateText?.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim() || null,
    email: emailText || null,
  };
}

async function run() {
  await ensureOutputDir();

  const browser = await webkit.launch();
  const page = await browser.newPage();
  await page.goto('https://ngodarpan.gov.in/#/search-ngo', {
    waitUntil: 'networkidle',
    timeout: 60000,
  });

  await selectDropdownOption(page, 'selectedState', SELECTIONS.selectedState);
  await page.waitForTimeout(1000);
  await selectDropdownOption(page, 'selectedDistrict', SELECTIONS.selectedDistrict);
  await selectMultiOptions(page, 'selectedSectors', SELECTIONS.selectedSectors);
  await selectMultiOptions(page, 'selectedNgoTypes', SELECTIONS.selectedNgoTypes);

  const captchaImageBase64 = await captureCaptcha(page);
  const captchaText = await decodeCaptchaText(captchaImageBase64);
  console.log('Decoded captcha text:', captchaText);
  await page.fill('#captchaInput', captchaText);

  const searchButton = await waitForSearchButtonEnabled(page);
  await searchButton.click();

  await page.waitForTimeout(5000);
  const tableLocator = page.locator('table').first();
  await tableLocator.waitFor({ state: 'visible', timeout: 60000 });
  await tableLocator.screenshot({ path: TABLE_SCREENSHOT_PATH });
  const tableData = await collectAllTableRows(page);

  let detailInfo = null;
  if (tableData.rows.length > 0) {
    try {
      await ensureFirstPageDisplayed(page);
      detailInfo = await captureDetailForFirstRecord(page);
    } catch (detailError) {
      console.warn('Detailed record capture failed:', detailError);
      detailInfo = null;
    }
  }

  fs.writeFileSync(
    TABLE_DATA_PATH,
    JSON.stringify(
      {
        capturedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        selections: SELECTIONS,
        table: {
          headers: tableData.headers,
          rows: tableData.rows,
          rowCount: tableData.rows.length,
        },
        assets: {
          captcha: CAPTCHA_PATH,
          tableScreenshot: TABLE_SCREENSHOT_PATH,
        },
      },
      null,
      2
    )
  );

  if (detailInfo) {
    fs.writeFileSync(
      DETAILED_RECORD_PATH,
      JSON.stringify(
        {
          capturedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          selections: SELECTIONS,
          table: {
            headers: tableData.headers,
            rowCount: tableData.rows.length,
            firstRow: tableData.rows[0],
          },
          detail: detailInfo,
        },
        null,
        2
      )
    );
    console.log(`Detail data for the first record written to ${DETAILED_RECORD_PATH}.`);
  } else {
    console.log('Detail data for the first record was not captured.');
  }

  console.log(`Table captured with ${tableData.rows.length} rows across all pages. Data written to ${TABLE_DATA_PATH}.`);
  await browser.close();
}

run().catch((err) => {
  console.error('Search workflow failed:', err);
  process.exit(1);
});
